Shanghai Local Supplement of Shen Bao (Shanghai Daily)

Talking Point

Doctors Have Started Soliciting Customers

— Meng Ruo

The large number of doctors in Shanghai can be seen from the signs hanging on various roads. Because there are many people in the medical profession, competition is inevitable in terms of business. The propaganda in the advertisements is naturally exaggerated. If you charge one dollar for an injection, I will offer a 50% discount and only charge 50 cents. If this family charges six dollars for delivery, that family will drastically reduce the price to four dollars. This situation seems to be very beneficial to patients. But in fact, it is not, it is precisely the misfortune of the patients.

However, although the business competition among hospitals is fierce, using the means of soliciting customers to grab business is a new fact that has only recently been discovered. A certain doctor specializes in hiring people to wait in front of major hospitals. When patients go to the hospital for treatment, they try to lure them away. This must be said to be a unique business technique. The impact of this is that the doctor's reputation will be damaged, and the patient will be greatly deceived.

The method of prevention should naturally be to strictly crack down on unlicensed hospitals. Because this kind of soliciting behavior is probably not something that legitimate doctors would do. Only some incompetent doctors can do it. Of course, even legitimate hospitals cannot guarantee that there are no people who only care about profit, but that is another matter.

However, the new fact that doctors are specializing in hiring people to solicit customers also shows the desolate situation of hospital business. Because the current market is affected by the economic downturn, and people's lives are becoming increasingly difficult. Most families cannot even maintain food and clothing, and they have no extra energy to take medicine when they are sick. This will greatly hit the general practitioners, and to the point that some people come out to grab business.

Prostitutes soliciting customers is common and not surprising. Now that doctors have also started soliciting customers, it is really strange. Running a hospital, instead of developing in a legitimate direction, actually uses the means of soliciting customers to grab business. It is possible that in the future, they will solicit from the road and solicit to the house, specializing in hiring people to seek patients from house to house.

Livelihood

— Zheng Mingliao

The sky quickly darkened, it was already night. It was still raining incessantly, dripping, dripping, hitting the broken tin roof, and flowing down from the rotten holes in the broken tin roof, dripping down the wall, drop by drop, onto the floor. The floor was like a street, shining brightly, reflecting the faint green light of the street lamp shining in from outside. The scene was very scary, as if it were like that in the underworld—if it were really in the underworld, that would be good. Lin Sheng had been looking for death and life all day long, but his young wife held him back, and his own little boy, who had just learned to walk at a little over two years old, also cried and dragged him down. As a result, Lin Sheng only shed a face full of tears, saying to them in a kind of indescribable cruel and resentful voice: "Alas! What do I owe you? Tell me! Why should I suffer so much!" He wished he could slam his head against the wall and die. But saying it over and over again, the young wife still said the same unchanging sentence in her wailing: "You...you can't go this way...look at me...for the sake of the child...you can't go this way...it doesn't matter if we are poor...we don't complain even if we starve to death...you can't go this way..."

So, Lin Sheng's heart was like a spoonful of molten lead poured into it, bursting and aching unbearably. The two people pulled and tugged each other, still collapsed on that only broken chair, panting urgently, like a tiger exhausted from fighting, and now, exhausted, everything had reached a dead end, and there was no more strength and courage to continue living.

"We don't complain even if we starve to death!" This voice pierced Lin Sheng's heart, aching especially unbearably. Yes, the family, old and young, had not eaten anything for two days, and "starving to death" was not far away. Warm tears flowed slowly on Lin Sheng's cheeks. He didn't know what kind of mood he had at this time.

"But, can it really be that we starve to death while we are still young?" Seeing the woman and child groaning weakly in hunger, and himself, himself with a healthy body that won't die, what can't he do? Go steal, go rob, also……

Thinking about it, Lin Sheng fell asleep in extreme stimulation and decline. The night was already very deep, the wind was howling outside, rolling up the dead leaves in the dark half-air, and then letting them fall into the puddles on the ground, floating like a rudderless canoe broken by huge waves in the sea……

The next day it was still raining. When Lin Sheng woke up from his deep sleep at dawn, his heart was completely calm. Like a death row inmate who has made a decision, everything that is coming will eventually come, and distress is futile. Looking at his wife and child, their sallow faces all had the tranquil look of sound sleep. Everything from last night was simply like a past nightmare, except for the stomach

Page 18

The hunger pangs were aching, and his head was a little dizzy. He couldn't find any trace of misery.

Lin Sheng had already decided: the fate of their family would be decided on this day. This day, he had to find a livelihood no matter what, even if it meant risking his life, no matter what……

He quietly got up and opened the door. The street was cold and quiet. It was still early, and there were very few pedestrians on the road. The sesame cake shop was baking sesame cakes, and the aroma almost made people faint. In a money exchange shop across the street, the clerks were counting copper coins, wrapping them into bundles and stacking them on the counter.

Lin Sheng stared fiercely at them, and suddenly, his heart beat very fast, and even his hands trembled! Those copper coins! Baked cakes! Livelihood! Wife and child! Death……! Everything was flying in his head like a swarm of flies. His hands trembled even more, but finally, like a madman, he rushed over and punched the clerk counting copper coins in the face, and then grabbed ten or so bundles of copper coins and ran towards the distance of the street.

The street immediately became disturbed. The clerks in the shop shouted and chased, and a large crowd of people rushed after them. Finally, the police came. Three or four people intercepted Lin Sheng in the middle of the road, and then the police came up and beat him hard, and handcuffed his hands.

"Tell me, how many times have you done this? Tell me the truth!"

"Sir! Master! I have never done it before, this is the first time! Livelihood! This is the last decision for livelihood……!"

"The first time? Do you think we are children? Haha, you are so good at denying it! If we don't give you a hard time, you won't be willing to tell the truth, let's go!"

With a "slap," he was slapped on the face, and four policemen dragged Lin Sheng away like a live pig. The street was still raining, very muddy, and messy footprints were left on the cobblestone road, and not far away, Lin Sheng knew, all kinds of tortures were waiting for him……

Mule Cart

— Lu Zhi

Every morning I am always disturbed by the dull sound of that mule cart. The countryside is a bit scarily quiet. Because it is quiet, a wooden-wheeled cart can wake me up. And what is even more annoying is the hoarse voice of the old man driving the cart:

"Damn it, you little devil, see if you get the whip. ……"

The sound of the whip was not heard hitting the mule, but was replaced by a heavy sigh.

That old man was nearly sixty years old. Squinting eyes, beard like weeds, face purplish-red, covered with gray-white beard, looking like Santa Claus, but he always seemed to be frowning, never smiling.

That mule was the same, so thin that its hock bones were like two horns standing on its hind legs, its head was always lowered listlessly, but it had the strength to endure. After the old man scolded it, it still dragged the rickety cart step by step.

The roads in the countryside are really difficult to walk, especially on rainy days. When you step on it with one foot, the mud immediately surrounds your foot. When you try to pull up your left foot, your right foot sinks even deeper. So when it rained at night, or when it was raining, the sound of the cart wheels was gone, but the old man's scolding was denser and louder. Also at this time, the sound of the whip was heard on the mule's back.

I hated it, and sometimes I was so angry that I put on my clothes and went to the window, wanting to curse him a few times. I tried a few times, but when I saw the old man wearing a torn piece of clothing, wearing a straw hat with a hole in it, holding the reins in one hand, and shaking the other hand and half of his body in the air, the cursing words always rolled back into my stomach. So early, the east was only a little white, the stars were shining high, and he had to drive the cart out. This scene made me unable to scold him. I stood blankly in front of the window, watching him try to drive the mule over the uneven road, to find food for him and the mule. Although I knew that if I got up at this time, I would have a headache all day today. I have a very bad habit, I can't sleep anymore once I get up in the morning. A day's work has no free time, just like that mule, working from morning to night.

Sometimes, when I had dinner around one or two o'clock, this old man would drive the cart back again. When driving the cart back, I often only heard the sound of the wheels rolling over the uneven road. He rarely scolded the mule. But sometimes, maybe business was bad, and the sound of the whip was very loud in the night sky.

The old man really only had him and the mule left. No children. One time he came back very early, and had eaten some wine, probably because business was good. I and two colleagues talked to him. He stopped the cart and shook his head on the driving platform. It was also at this time that I saw his eyes, which were full of sorrow. Even in this moment of triumph, he couldn't get rid of his sorrow.

"I have several children, the oldest would be... (he counted) nearly forty now, and the youngest would be twenty years old. ... I feel a little regret now, I didn't have a daughter, they are all boys, four, you gentlemen think, how blessed... Several of them have gone to eat rations, and they left and never came back, leaving me, this dry old man, and this mule. It is this mule that is so hard to keep. Those who eat rations wanted to pull it away. I hid it in a mountain cave. Really, I think about it now, I shouldn't have let my children go to eat rations. What Sun Marshal, Lu Marshal, have gold and silver, but I, an old man, only have a bare body now. I still rely on this mule. It is more useful than my sons! ... It's not early, gentlemen, I'm going to let this animal graze!" As he said this, he drove the cart away again.

Sometimes when I think of this gray-haired little mule, I congratulate it. It has the old man's love, but we work like mules from day to night, only having emptiness and loneliness.

I endured the sound of the mule cart for half a year, and now I haven't heard the sound of wooden wheels and the old man's scolding with love for a long time, and I feel lonely. Is he still healthy now?

A Farm Scene

— Luo

Winter brings a delightful sun.

On the threshing ground, tall stacks of firewood have already been piled high. It's another year of bountiful harvest, temporarily easing the farmers' furrowed brows that have been locked tight for a year. However, the daily trips to town to inquire about "market prices" leave a dreadful impression deep in their hearts! "Grain prices are worthless!" Perhaps they mourn the ox they sold off and become sorrowful.

Sparrows, like little children, hop and skip around on the threshing ground. They have been waiting somewhere, somehow, for a year, and now, shaking their mottled hemp clothing, their pointed yellow beaks peck at each pure white grain of rice, a sumptuous feast!

In the fields, rice roots remain, clump after clump, so neatly arranged, letting the sun shine everywhere. Standing on the field and looking ahead, the field ridges resemble waistbands, cinching the square fields, extending all the way to the edge of the sky; there, pale gray clouds float.

Far away by the riverbank, there is a cart shed for oxen, newly thatched with fresh reeds, glistening in the sun. Inside the shed, it is quiet and still, with only the creaking sound of the wind passing through the pulley. The old ox, toiling tirelessly all year round, is tethered beneath a tree—now is its time to rest. It has just finished a hearty meal of reeds, turning its long, slender eyes towards the shed, perhaps wondering, after drawing water for so many years, enduring so many whips from the herdboy, how it can't escape this narrow shed?

Under the sun, the farm women sit in a sheltered spot. Some are mending clothes for their children, others are weaving new straw shoes for their husbands to wear to town. In their hearts, they also harbor a hope, hoping that the price of rice will rise, so that when they sell at a good price, they can buy a fashionable new dress for the New Year. This hope has been there for more than a year or two; they are still wearing the clothes they wore when they got married!

Naturally, the happiest are the children. They pester their mothers for fried broad beans, and everyone takes a handful, hides them in their pockets, and gathers in the corner of the threshing ground to draw tortoise shell diagrams, using the broad beans to wager.

Under this delightful sun, we have not seen a single farmer spend a leisurely afternoon there, only white-haired old men smoking cheap dry tobacco, reminiscing about their golden age!

Those farmers whose skin has been tanned purple by the venomous summer sun now gather in small teahouses in the market towns, hoping to turn each grain they planted into money to repay debts, celebrate the New Year, and buy a new dress for their wives at a satisfying "market price." Their hearts, like the pulley in the cart shed, spin endlessly.

The sun, after a day's journey, is sent back by the crows' cawing, and wisps of black smoke rise from the thatched roofs of every house. Another day passes, and the New Year draws closer.

The Wife Has Gone to Be a Wet Nurse

— By Zhang Jingxia

In the Carriage

— Luo Yu

The early spring air, trapped inside the carriage, mingled with the pungent smell of cigarettes, becoming stifling.

Their bodies, tossed about by the high speed, were squeezed between two reclining seats. The afternoon sun peeked through the window, trembling restlessly, teasing their hands and knees, then shifting from one face to another.

At the doorway, a young man in a railway uniform greeted his colleague in the gentle accent of Tangshan, then calmly walked back into the carriage. He walked to the side of three women.

"Who was that you were talking to?"

"A colleague nearby, also from the same hometown."

The woman, who looked to be in her forties, answered the man in uniform. She had the compassionate face of a missionary, and a pair of ever-compassionate eyes. Those eyes tirelessly searched among the mountains and trees, as if seeing some buried happiness there.

"Aunt? Take a look over there. My father works in that town." The young man had sat down to her right, pointing towards the foot of the distant mountain by the window, and spoke like this. There was a blurry cedar forest over there, with a layer of miasma lingering, and a dark boundary underneath, with the roofs of pine houses vaguely visible at one end.

Three pairs of eyes longingly looked over.

The young man's face, recently shaven, looked very bright in front of the window. He had a pair of prominent large eyes, and a slightly protruding mouth, making him look like an alert and careful young man. He kept flashing a few smiles, gazing at the delicate face of the bride across from him.

She was his newly married wife, and they were about to settle down in a new town at the end of the railway line ahead.

The woman dressed in bright clothes looked constantly worried and didn't talk much, sitting there thinking. The reflection from the carriage roof shone on her powdered face, creating a trembling purple color. Her younger brother was sleeping on her lap. Her mother, a fat woman, buried her face in her left shoulder, snoring heavily.

"We'll be home before dark," the young man in uniform said to himself, as if comforting her, stretching his back.

"Call Peng-ge when you get home and have him come see us tonight," the aunt said to the young man, her eyes brushing over the reddish-brown rocky slopes.

"He can't come. Are you hoping he'll come with the train tonight?" The man paused for a moment and said, "That colleague just told me that Peng-ge has gone to the hospital."

"What, does that mean his illness has gotten worse?!" The anxious mother asked. The man paused for a moment and said:

"His numbness is unchanged, (but his right hand is completely unable to move after getting angry). That colleague said his eyesight is failing. One time, his sister-in-law hit his head against the wall, making him unable to raise his hand, and then his eyes started having problems. He saw him at the station one evening, and asked, 'Why don't you go home?' But he didn't answer the first question. When he looked again, he realized that he was struggling there, waiting in pain; he only said, 'I can't see clearly anymore, older brother'." He stopped there, seeing the change in the aunt's face, an expression of restraint after prolonged sobbing.

"But luckily, Stationmaster Gangtian is treating him well, asking him to do less work, and also helping him treat his eyes, and there are also fellow villagers."

The aunt seemed to be falling into a dreamlike impasse, her lips trembling, wanting to say something, but it was very difficult.

At this moment, the woman across from her suddenly spoke.

"I heard that sister-in-law has been to school."

This sentence made the aunt very uneasy. But the husband answered with his youthful frankness:

"Studied? Even if there was such a thing, it wouldn't change her nature. She's just arguing with brother-in-law for no reason. Mom always says brother-in-law has a really good temper: he says there are so many girls around the railway, but he just happened to meet this female fortress owner, and she even gave brother-in-law several letters."

The bride smiled when she heard this; then she drooped her eyelids again with a faint sadness. She looked even more worried than before.

The aunt kept listening attentively to the conversation between the two young ones, but she kept her eyes fixed on the woman's fair face, which made her both bury her head and blush.

A deep sadness flashed through the aunt's eyes. She felt very flustered for a moment, seeing something dazzling flowing on that fair but not very beautiful female face.

Ballad Singing

Cao Xiaoying "Yu Qingting"

China-West (1040) 1 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "National Heroes" (By Gao Yangshanren)

The situation fluctuates and opinions vary. The people's morale declines and foreign powers are strong. China originally rose from the Kunlun Mountains. Moving east from the Xia and Shang dynasties. The Zhou Dynasty lasted eight hundred years. Conferring titles on the royal family to the four borders. The Central Plains gradually expanded. The barbarians were reduced to wasteland. There were many miracles in the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods. The Qin Dynasty unified through conquest. The tyranny was truly autocratic. Liu Bang rose up by slaying the serpent. Seeking justice for the people to destroy Qin and Chu. Relying only on Han Xin, Xiao He, and Zhang Liang. Transmitting the throne for five generations to establish the emperor. At that time, the Eastern Kou Hui were very powerful and violent. Raping, plundering, and doing everything. Coastal residents lacked peace and prosperity. Fertile land became desolate. A thousand miles of plains became a wasteland. National heroes rose in time. Appointing generals and ministers like Huo Guang. Killing them so that their ships were broken, their masts were destroyed, and their heads fell. Their souls scattered and fled to the ocean. From then on, the border people enjoyed peace and prosperity. There is still a temple on the coast today. The name of the great general is known far and wide. His fame will last ten thousand ages.

He Yunfang, He Qinfang "Double Pearl Ball"

Yuan Chang (1120) 3:30 PM to 4:15 PM

Opening "New Opening on Wealth, Nobility, Poverty, and Lowliness"

All are born after ten months of pregnancy. Heaven is extremely fair. Who knows that the social situation changes? Distinguishing between wealth, nobility, poverty, and lowliness, importance and lightness. The wealthy have limitless wealth that is difficult to calculate. Gold, silver, and jewels fill boxes. Numerous high halls and large houses. Calling servants and prostitutes to cook food and drink. Buying good fields and taking the rent. Regardless of the bankruptcy of farmers who want to resort to violence. The noble have power and influence to deceive others. Completely disregarding reason and reputation. Never thinking that snow pillars and ice mountains are difficult to last. Their family property will be sacrificed in the future. The most bitter is the situation of the common people, who are extremely poor. No way to appeal and making no sound. Exhausting all efforts to maintain, with depleted mental and physical strength. It is pitiful to have land but not be able to cultivate it. Some suddenly have suicidal thoughts due to failure. Hanging themselves or jumping into the water to end their lives. I think that Confucius of Mount Ni was unmatched. He said that equality means no poverty, which is very clear. Unfortunately, no one follows this. Resulting in a division of classes into disgrace and honor. In the future, after equality and freedom. Treating everyone as brothers equally. Only then can we see a clear world.

Jiang Binchu "Three Smiles"

New Sound (1380) 7 PM to 8 PM

Opening "Yun San's Suicide"

Red Mansion Dreams speak of absurdity. Unlucky beauties are very sad. Yun Sanjie has, a moon-like face and flower-like appearance, with an iron-like heart. Relying on others to helplessly spend her years. Meeting Liu Lang, a talented and romantic man. Named Xiang Lian, with a strong personality. They are, as if they had known each other before. Giving a treasure to seal their marriage. Considered to be. A talented man and a beautiful woman, an unparalleled couple. Entrusting their lives to each other forever. Who knows, a storm suddenly arises out of nowhere. Slanderous words enter her ears and regret is difficult to bear. Liu Lang demands back the mandarin duck sword. Sanjie, her heart aches to the point of breaking. Drawing out the green blade, it flashes like lightning. Pointlessly committing suicide on the spot. Peach blossom blood splatters on her clothes. Startling Xiang Lian into losing his composure. From then on, he let his hair grow long and went into the mountains to cultivate the Dao. Eliminating worldly obstacles to answer San Niang. The twelve golden hairpins are all enchanting. Only San Niang has a strong personality. A mound of yellow earth buries Hengtang.

Movie News

Beauty

"Eternal Smile" Theme Song

Green willows under Zijin Mountain,

Iron hooves and silver bells,

Accompany the singing of beauty, every sound passing by the future,

The mountains and rivers of the Qinhuai River are cold,

Pale moon and sparse stars,

Causing beauty to worry, every thought reaching dawn.

Beauty, like beautiful people, a deep affection,

Knowing me is like the green willow,

Suffering for you, bitterness is also willing.

Beauty, like beautiful people, a deep affection,

Knowing me is like the clear water,

Dying for you, death is also peaceful.

According to this song, it was written by Zeng Yan and has been composed by the film director Wu Cun, sung by the lead actress Hu Die, and recorded by the Baidai Company.

"Midnight Song" Cast

The candidates for the main roles in "Midnight Song" are Jin Shan, Gu Er'yi, Shi Chao, Xiao Ying, Gu Menghu, etc. for the male role, and Hu Ping, Zhou Wenzhu, Xu Manli, Chen Yun, etc. for the female role. All are very famous and well-accomplished artists. Hu Ping is expected to play a daughter of a wealthy family who has suffered deep trauma. The internal performance in several scenes is beautiful, giving people a sense of sadness, purity, and beauty, creating a unique style.

"Little Aunt" Chen Qixia

Hua'an Broadcasting

Hua'an's new film "United China Symphony", already completed; there are Zhu Shilin's "Ghost", He Zhifu's "Moonlit Landscape", Shen Fu's "Three People", Tan Youliu's "Stormy Night", Situ Huimin's "Two Mao Coins", Sun Yu's "Madman's Rhapsody" and other segments. Others such as Fei Mu's "Spring Boudoir Broken Dream" and Cai Chusheng's "Little Five Righteous", are in production.

Wang Cilong's "Lonely City Martyr" has been completed. The sound, light, acting skills are excellent. In the film, Chen Yanyan and Han Langen both play peddlers. Yanyan sells peanuts, Han sells spiced tea eggs, and speaks Shandong dialect, with many gimmicks.

He Mengfu's "Daughter of the General" has been very busy with filming in recent days. The scene of the secret underground room of the party members is ingenious in structure and cannot be handled without those familiar with revolutionary work.

Shen Fu's "Match Made in Heaven" is now four-fifths complete, and most of it will be completed soon. Han Langen has as many gimmicks as Chaplin in "Modern Times". Filming has been temporarily suspended due to Bai Lang's illness.

Tan Youliu directed the "Stormy Night" segment in "United China Symphony", developing the greed of a miser. Because of his habit of loving money as his life, he unknowingly released the enemy who killed his only son. Zheng Junli, Bai Lu, and Liu Qiong co-star.

He Mengfu directed "Moonlit Landscape" in "United China Symphony" using a sketch method. The famous ancient musician Sha Mei composed the music. The song title "Our Home" has a tragic and strong spirit, and will be collected into a record by Shambart Company.

Sun Yu directed the "Madman's Rhapsody" in "United China Symphony". Shan Shangwu played a mad farmer, acting extremely hard, and therefore achieved excellent results.

"Venus" Issue 8 Bestseller

The Venus pictorial, hosted by the Wang Cilong brothers, has become even richer in its eighth issue and was shipped from Tianjin to Shanghai a few days ago. A new batch of 5,000 copies has been added by the local agent distributor. Those who wish to buy it should not miss the opportunity. The catalog of this issue is as follows: cover in three-color edition of Chen Yanyan's recent photos, and recent photos of stars such as Hu Die, Yuan Meiyun, Tan Ying, Ye Qiuxin, Ye Wenqiu, and Liu Liying, and many stills of recently produced films by major film companies. In addition, there are also inscriptions of celebrities, current affairs, family, romance, drama, comics, and other works, as well as sketches. The eight horses of Zhang Daqian brothers are the most brilliant in painting and calligraphy. The entire book is printed on heavy-weight Daolin paper and sells for only 15 cents per copy. All bookstores and newsstands are selling them on consignment. Contributions are also welcome. Mailing address: Wang Jielong, No. 37, Jianye Lane, Fuli Road, French Concession.
